<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f4da9e0a-fa88-41b1-8eac-b05bc91615a2'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">قرأتها خلال يومين( واظن ضغط نفسي )<br/>كنت متحمس ليها جدا متأثر ومنغمس في الاحداث ومع الابطال <br/>في الحقيقة نقلت الكاتبة الاحداث ببراعه وبتفاصيل كتيرة ومنطقية<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">قرأتها خلال يومين( واظن ضغط نفسي )<br />كنت متحمس ليها جدا متأثر ومنغمس في الاحداث ومع الابطال <br />في الحقيقة نقلت الكاتبة الاحداث ببراعه وبتفاصيل كتيرة ومنطقية جدا وعذبتنا مع رغد طول الرواية <br />لكن في اخر 500 صفحة بدأت امل من كتر الضغط والضيق نتيجة تفاعلي بالاحداث وكل ما اقول خلاص سينتهى العذاب وندخل مرحلة جديدة من الحب والفرح القي الموضوع تعقد اكثر <br />لكن اعترف انى استمتعت واتسال ليه الروايات الجميلة كتلك لا تتحول الي مسلسل <br />تقيمي ثلاثة نجمات <br />والسبب هو النهاية التعيسة التى لم تشفي غليلي توقعت مقدار اكتر من عرض مشاعر وليد ورغد وكيف الحال عندما صار حبيبين <br />كنت محتاج جرعة من الرومانسية بصراحه =D <br />وكمان نهاية سامر واروي في القصة غابت ولم تتضح بوضوح وهما كانوا شخصيات ارتبط بهما <br />صحيح شكرا للكاتبة علي التزامها بقدر كبير من تعاليم دينينا <br />وكنت اود ان استفسر لما لم تذكري اسم البلد التى وقعت بها الاحداث ؟<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

  <span id="freeText5556392618754680233" style="display:none">the biggest disappointment i had reading this novel is that it had so much potential but the author just walked through them all without taking the chance to get into the deeper shade of the story, the fundamental dew of the story is strong but the aspects the author chose to talk the story through were extremely poor, i mean it's freaking 1600 pages long and she could easily have gone through some more relatable issues like war, arranged marriages, political prisoners and life in jail .. plus there were some important events the author didn't bother describing like samer's feeling after the breakup, how he got his parents' dead bodies and how he got involved in that assasins group .. her description of the characters was artificial and one-sided for example you find that ra3'ad is childish and dana is always jealous, while it's part of the human nature to have multiple sides and shades to your character like when you act with jealousy it's not because you a jealous person but it's because you have insecurities and the author should've focused on the insecurity part rather than just the jealousy :( <br /><br />the language was poor and i didn't like the way she chose to tell the story through (i found it extremely cheesy) not mentioning the mistakes there are in saying the wrong names at the wrong parts and jumping from telling the story from one person's perspective into another's without giving the reader a clue about the change that happened :\ <br />it was stressful reading someone's feelings and not knowing who you're reading about</span>

  <span id="freeText2178983597433842102" style="display:none">Book 1:<br /><br />4.9 stars because at some point I hated the main characters...<br /><br />Now, I know this is an Arabic book and I should be writing my review in Arabic but it's one am right now and my book brain isn't functioning properly. <br /><br />Plot: SO MANY PLOT TWISTS AAAAHHHHH and why is everyone in the story making up a far-from-what's-happening conclusion about things?? And just WHY was I hooked from the first page?? So many questions that I have no answer to..<br /><br />This book was very thrilling because it was so realistic and not in any way cheesy!! I also really liked it because this is the first book ever that I read from Arab-Muslim POV characters which made me feel so relatable and at ease with the characters and setting. <br /><br />My book-reading record is now 517 pages in 24 hours. 24 hours went like this: 12AM to 3AM and then one hour the next morning and then continued the book from 9PM to 12PM. <br /><br />Songs for this book: Warzone -The Wanted<br /> Show me love -The Wanted<br /> Angel with a shotgun -The Cab<br /><br />Book 2:<br /><br />Ok this book was such an emotional roller coaster. I had to clear that up. There were so many (complex) plot twists, the characters were also highly complex which is wow and I must say I absolutely loved this book and can you believe I read two 500page books in two days??? Personally I am amazed and scared at how gripping this book was!<br /><br />Overall, I loved this book and ESPECIALLY the ending. Very satisfying. Lots of huge plot twists! A romance novel in such a non-cheesy and extremely realistic! Simply awesome.<br /><br />Recommending this to anyone who can read Arabic or can learn and then read Arabic :)<br /><br />-T</span>

  <span id="freeText2044064980375222262" style="display:none">is there such a pure love, such a platonic love. I would say it's just in fiction. I started the book expecting more changes, stories, events, but I think it's all about love and crime, crime and love, then rivality between the two brothers, Raghad and her cousin then between Raghad and arwa. <br />I don't know what happened when Ammar kidnapped Raghad that motivate walid to kill him. After 800 pages, I still feel like some parts of the book are just repetition or are just accessories. I don't read a lot modern books in arabic language, but I really enjoy all arabic books. I think the book don't show the real passion, it's still conservative, I guess because of the author's society or what. But it's still a good book. <br /></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wZ4BpFb3Qyzmej4st3dZhTxkW3kY8Y4cH7BpDuOzo04TF3y0OnCMgHXctHYyHF+RQYRelRsUF9J9bKLtmXRD+w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MI0AaIJyvtvTbCDHgYTBSDHz7/oy8wj73xYpVD2cMCziBH147vVxd0DKqp0E78dcTBPqFjEWkTW9yuK3R1vQmQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
